The reason we test games in CPU reviews at lower resolutions such as 720p and below is simple; titles are more likely to be CPU bound than they are GPU bound at lower resolutions. This means there are more frames for the processor to process as opposed to the graphics card doing the majority of the heavy lifting. What is negative reinforcement in operant conditioning?

28 Jul 2024, 00:00

Negative reinforcement aims to increase specific behaviors by removing negative consequences or stimuli. It is part of the operant conditioning theory of learning. This theory also includes positive reinforcement, which increases behaviors through rewards. What is the meaning of negative reinforcement? Negative reinforcement is a method that can be used to help teach specific behaviors. With negative reinforcement, something uncomfortable or otherwise unpleasant is taken away in response to a stimulus.

Tonal shading is used by designers to assist differentiate which sides of a drawing will be exposed to the sun the most, as well as to enhance the appearance of the artwork and ‚Äúmake‚Äù it seem more 3D. To put it another way, what makes tonal sketching so effective? While linear drawing encourages the establishment of boundaries, tonal drawing seeks to dissolve these boundaries while emphasising the quality of light and atmosphere that links all things in the viewer‚Äôs field of vision.

Programming languages seem to be cyclical. Low level languages give developers the chance to have very fast code with the minimum of commands necessary, but the closer you code to hardware the more difficult it becomes, and the developer should have a good grasp of the hardware in order to get the best performance.
